AUTHOR     (B.H.Patrick, M.G.Schomberg, M.G.Sowerby, J.E.Jolly)   2000200100007 
            Jolly only for 66PARIS,2,117.                         2000200100008 
TITLE      -Average values of the fission cross section and alpha 2000200100009 
            for 94-Pu-239 in the neutron energy range 100 eV to   2000200100010 
            30 keV.- (EANDC(UK)-96),                              2000200100011 
           -Measurements of ETA, alpha and neutron cross-sections 2000200100012 
            for 94-Pu-239 on the Harwell neutron time-of-flight   2000200100013 
            spectrometer.- (66PARIS,2,117).                       2000200100014 
FACILITY   (LINAC,2UK HAR) 45 MeV Harwell electron linear accel.  2000200100015 
INC-SOURCE (PHOTO)    Photo neutrons from booster target used,    2000200100016 
            neutron pulse width (immoderated) = 220 ns.           2000200100017 
SAMPLE     Three samples of 2.9 inch diameter contained in        2000200100018 
             3.0 inch diameter 12 inch long aluminum cylinders.   2000200100019 
            1.8% 94-Pu-240 for  N = 0.02433 at/b,                 2000200100020 
            1.8% 94-Pu-240 for  N = 0.00440 at/b  and             2000200100021 
            3.2% 94-Pu-240 for  N = 0.00115 at/b.                 2000200100022 
METHOD     (TOF,TRN)  Time of flight paths = 97.55 m and 34.9 m,  2000200100023 
                      timing channel width = 125 ns.              2000200100024 
DETECTOR   (BF3,NAICR)  Liquid scintillator with pulse shape      2000200100025 
            discrimination against gamma radiation for fission    2000200100026 
            yield measurements, boron-10 slab viewed by Na-I      2000200100027 
            crystals for neutron spectrum measurements and        2000200100028 
           (GLASD)    Lithium loaded glass detectors for both     2000200100029 
            neutron spectrum measurements and transmission        2000200100030 
            measurements.                                         2000200100031 
ANALYSIS   .Measured transmission, fission neutron yield and      2000200100032 
            neutron spectrum.                                     2000200100033 
           .Sigma(total) derived from transmission.               2000200100034 
           .Eta derived from transmission, yield (corrected for   2000200100035 
            single elastic scattering) and the neutron spectrum.  2000200100036 
           .Sigma(fission) derived from normalized ETA and        2000200100037 
            sigma(total) using    sigma(fission) =                2000200100038 
             eta*(sigma(total)-sigma(scattering))/nu-bar(prompt), 2000200100039 
            assuming nu-bar(prompt) = 2.864 (constant) and taking 2000200100040 
            for sigma(scattering) an estimate based on resonance  2000200100041 
            parameters (BNL-325,2nd ed,Suppl.2 and KFK-120/1/1V3) 2000200100042 
            and on sigma(potential) = 10.3+-0.5 b (C.A.Uttley,    2000200100043 
            EANDC(UK)-40 l ,unpublished).                         2000200100044 
MONITOR    (94-PU-239(N,ABS),,ETA)                                2000200100045 
                  Normalized between 65.39 eV and                 2000200100046 
            65.94 eV to ETA = 1.547+-3% which was found           2000200100047 
            by the low energy measurement.                        2000200100048 
           .This measurement was normalized at 10.95 eV to ETA =  2000200100049 
            2.041 (F.D.Brooks et al.,AERE-M-1709(1966)),          2000200100050 
           .which itself has been normalized at thermal energy.   2000200100051 
           .Sigma(fission) has been normalized through eta.       2000200100052 
COMMENT    .Measurements performed in two runs                    2000200100053 
             10 eV to  1 keV, resolution = 7.2 ns/m and           2000200100054 
             50 eV to 30 keV, resolution = 2.5 ns/m.              2000200100055 
           .Because of resolution and self screening effects are  2000200100056 
            given only the average values of sigma(fission) for   2000200100057 
            the lower energy experiment and the data for the      2000200100058 
            higher energy experiment, both above 100 eV.          2000200100059 
CORRECTION .Background subtracted using black resonance technique.2000200100060 
            Permanent resonance filters are                       2000200100061 
            low energy run  sodium, high energy run  aluminium.   2000200100062 
           .Corrected for single elastic scattering in sample     2000200100063 
            (high Z), sample impurities (low Z)  and in the       2000200100064 
            aluminium windows of the sample container.            2000200100065

            background,                                           2000200200012 
           .Uncertainty in the resonance part of sigma(scattering)2000200200013

            than 4% in the result,                                2000200200015 
           .Errors due to multiple in stead of single scattering  2000200200016 
            a few per cent,                                       2000200200017
